msg:After the previous Sheraton was delisted, it became Sofitel under the French Accor Group.

It is located in the CBD of Qingnian Street, walking to Metro Line 2 City Library Station, and also very close to K11.

The design of the hotel is rooted in the French concept of enjoying life, combining French romance and decorativeism, with a magnificent side and a sense of avant-garde design.

The old hotel has been renovated, and the pattern has not changed much, but it still has a strong taste of old money. The spiral staircase and crystal chandeliers in the lobby are in brilliant tones and have a sense of age.

The room is decorated with Sofitel's typical blue and purple, with log color and gold, which makes people feel comfortable. The velvet chaise longue is comfortable to look at, the background wall is a combination of geometric lines full of design, and the bedside lamp adopts a chandelier pattern which is very interesting.


The bathroom is dry and wet, and the spare parts are Lanvin, which is the mainstay of Sofitel.


The price starting from 500 yuan is already very cost-effective for business hotels in Shenyang.


Good service from Sally and Daisy in the cafeteria.
